< text>
Boyfriend and I were pleasantly surprised to find no wait and clean tables on a Saturday morning. The menu is limited and delicious: he had the Rhea's Breakfast with eggs cooked exactly to his liking, and I had the Rhea's Breakfast Sandwich. Both come with potatoes and they were AWESOME. I feel like we got a lot of food, especially for the price - we'll definitely be back. Side note: they do not accept AmEx and there's a minimum for cards so splitting checks might not work.< /text>

<rating>5</rating>< Text>
Rhea's has extremely great brunch food, and with no wait at 12:30 pm on a Saturday.  I got the normal brunch food (eggs, bacon, toast) and it was delicious.

I asked for wheat bread, and they ran out and so I had sourdough, but during the middle of the brunch our waitress came back and gave me wheat bread because she knew I explicitly asked for it. Great service!<//Text>

< Review>
The wait time around lunch can be a bit long. But all food is cooked to order - nothing is cooked ahead of time, and you can even watch for yourself while sitting at the counter.

The buttermilk fried chicken sandwiches have more crispy, delicious chicken packed onto a bun than I thought was possible.<//Review>

The food was so good I forgot to take pictures during our scarf time but was able to capture my left over Tokyo fried rice.

<date>1410997998122< /date><GmapID>0x80c2dab70b5bcfbf:0x1cb85972ba0e7378<//GmapID><rating>4< /rating><name>Sally Elbassir<//name><Response>None< /Response><Review>Came here on Sunday night and was surprised to find it really busy! Initially we were seated at a table with bar stools before moving to a booth. Most people come for the alcoholic boba, but I was there for the sushi and I was starving!

My friends and I split the spicy tuna pizza app, and then hungry me ordered the spicy tuna roll, monkey brains, and shrimp tempura roll. It was a LOT of food, but I ended up paying a little less than $30. Not bad at all!

Spicy tuna rice pizza: Delish. I am a huge fan of spicy tuna with crispy rice, and the 'pizza' was no exception.

Spicy tuna roll: Hard to mess up, but the tuna was fresh. The roll fell apart a bit as I was grabbing pieces with chopsticks, but that's really my only complaint.

Monkey brains: this was half an avocado with crabmeat and tempura. It came out last so I was a bit full, but honestly I think it needed a tad more seasoning. The slight blandness of the avocado overwhelmed the crab a bit.

Shrimp tempura: One can never go wrong with deep fried shrimp in a roll right? 'Nuff said.

Service was hit and miss. The food generally came out quickly enough, but it was hard to get water refills and the waitress' attention.

Overall, good sushi place. I don't go to San Gabriel often, but would definitely eat here again if I were in the area.< /Review></record></dataset><record>

It use to be just weekends, it is now extended to Thurs-Sat I believe, but just call ahead so you won't be disappointed. Also, every weekday they have a special. Our waiter and waitress seemed nervous at first and it was a bit awkward because this was our first time here. We were disappointed a finding out we couldn't get alcohol-boba drinks and then they were also out of oysters! Agh!! We want our raw seafood, otherwise why go to a sushi joint?

Anyways, being super hungry I just ordered a few yakitori. We had the pork belly, squid, quail egg, and chicken hearts to start with. All of which were cooked very well. My friend was like why is this squid so soft? I thought it should be chewy! I told her that no, that squid is chewy if its overcooked, but this were perfectly grilled. Just FYI Yakitori on Wednesdays are $1.50 each!  I want to come back and eat grilled meats to my hearts content.

The sashimi/sushi here is average. I base this on the freshness and tastiness of the Ikura. I know, maybe thats not fair, but if its fresh I think other things are also. Whatever, don't tell me how to think! My ikura was bright and not wrinkly, not too salty, not too much rice, and did not taste too fishy.

We ordered sashimi plate for 2 people with 3 pieces of salmon, tuna, a white fish rolled around some sprouts, and what I believe was 3 pieces of yellow tail. It was plated very well and everything was fresh tasting. We had a piece of fatty salmon at the end and that was also delightful.

At the end of our meal the waiter that kept coming around was very nice and we asked if we could get ice cream for checking in on a app. He said yes, but they ran out of green tea. I was going to be annoyed again with this, but he saved the day offering other flavors with chocolate syrup and a cookie. That is the way to make me happy after running out of a 3rd item! (Even if its free...) So my friend and I had our dessert and then the owner came out and offered us each (and all the customers) pieces of lotus seed moon cake because it was the Moon Festival that week. <rate>5<//rate>< Text>
I have been in the area for a bit and finally came in and I am glad I did. The place has a very authentic feel, unlike some kind of chain, you always can tell with a family operated restaurant like this. It isn't surprising that it has been around for so many years. I had one of the best chicken salad meals from Art's in recent memory, everything was very fresh and well prepared. One of the best in The Valley. Great free parking set up, super convenient and easy to navigate. Very hearty portions at a great price and the chicken was very good, there are a lot of fresh options to decide on. The service was clean and fast and the takeout is really streamlined as well, they gave me some advice on how to do things next time to make it even better with the ordering, very nice people. Everything was great with nothing bad to report about my visit, others should visit and experience the quality themselves.< /Text>

< rate>
5<//rate>
< Text>
Finally got to check this place out! I've lived in the area and seen this place a million times, and today I finally made it.

I tried the Italian cold cut, a pretty simple choice that I find is a good way to see how good a sub place is. It was delicious! Perfect balance of meat, cheese, veggies and condiments. Bread was really good too.

Things to know before ordering:
1. The prices are the same for every sub they have. Get whatever you want!
2. The 8 inch (small) is the same amount of food as if you added an extra 2 inches to a Subway 6 in. and added double meat. Honestly, you get a lot more bang for your buck here than you do at Subway, and with way better taste. I ordered the 12 in. and it was a bit too much. Save that one for a large appetite.

Looking forward to coming here again and trying another option :)< /Text>
